NYIS BRGYA SO BRGYAD, NGA PA LA SPYOD 'JUG DAR tIKA RGYAL SRAS
'JUG NGOGS LA BRGYA DANG RE GSUM, TSAD MA MDO KUN BTUS DAR tIKA
MTHAR 'DZIN GDUNG SEL LA

BRGYA DANG NYER DRUG TSAD MA'I BRJED BYANG CHEN MO LA ZHE GSUM,

SGRIG THEG CHEN SGO 'BYED LA NYER BZHI, RNAM 'GREL THAR LAM GSAL
BYED

MA'I SNYING PO LA BCU BZHI, TSAD MA'I LAM tIKA LA NYER GNYIS,
'GAL

BZHI BCU ZHE BRGYAD, CHA PA LA RNAM 'GREL THAR LAM GSAL BYED LA
BZHI BRGYA DANG BRGYAD,

JA PA LA RTZA SHE DKA' GNAD LA BCO BRGYAD, TSAD MA RNAM NGES DAR
tIKA LA SUM BRGYA BCU BDUN, NYA PA LA TSAD MA RNAM NGES DAR tIK
DGONGS PA RAB GSAL LA NYIS

GNYIS
